# P15 LACMA Gothic Cathedral Ultra-Dense 10x Perspective Data

P15 tests a 10x increase in measurement/reference density. It is an experiment and does not replace the cleaner P13/P14 boards unless visually approved.

- Source page: https://collections.lacma.org/node/229641
- Source image URL: https://collections-images.lacma.org/images/13736/13736-1-primary.webp
- Source file: `SourceAssets/Reference/PerspectiveDrawing/WebReferences/REF_Perspective_GothicCathedral_LACMA_229641.webp`
- Density multiplier: `10x` for Hough caps, VP caps, and visible axis-reference targets.

## Full cathedral 10x
- Focus: global scaffold and primary depth solve
- Crop: `(0.01, 0.015, 0.99, 0.985)`
- Processing width/height: `2400 x 1838`
- Edge percentile: `95.15`
- Hough line cap: `2600`
- VP candidate cap: `280`
- Edge pixels: `52229`
- Hough lines kept: `719`
- Displayed axes: `47` X, `152` Y, `160` Z
- Solved VP: `(0.614990, 0.604815)`
- Z residual mean/max: `100.989px` / `218.765px`
